To help small businesses who’ve been hit hard by COVID-19, we created the Canada Emergency Commercial Rent Assistance. Together with the provinces and territories, we’ll provide forgivable loans to landlords so they can reduce rent for small business tenants by 75%. If you’re a landlord, and you and your tenant are eligible, you can apply for this benefit starting Monday, May 25th. For more details on the support we’re offering, and to find out what information you’ll need for your application, click here:

    ***BIG ANNOUNCEMENT*** •PART 1• Before I start, I know a lot of people hate me and I’m fine with that. I do not know what I have exactly said or done to these people, but a lot of people just don’t like me and I’ve accepted that and have grown from it. So... First off, I would like to wish myself a very Happy Birthday and thank all the people who have wished me so far. Anyway... Remember when I went to Doha - Qatar, Karachi/Islamabad - Pakistan, Mumbai - India and Dhaka/Cox’s Bazar - Bangladesh back in October? I didn’t really reveal who I worked for/with. Well, I went to work for/with National Geographic. It was honestly and seriously an honour working with them on set everyday for a week. I am so thankful for the opportunity. I earned about $20,000 USD, but the best part of the job wasn’t the pay. The best part of the job was connecting with my fellow filmmakers and peers on this work trip. Aside from the connections and references, I met a lot of professionals in the film industry, gained a ton of experience and knowledge. You know what else I’m grateful for? This trip was paid in-full. I didn’t have to pay for my flights, hotels, food, transportation/travel expenses and I received a $10,000 USD bonus compensation just last week for all my work. At this time, I would just like to express all my gratitude towards you all and especially God, Allah. Today, I am in that same exact position. My flights, hotels, food, transportation/travel expenses are fully paid for. I am and will be only paying for my chilling, leisure and tourism expenses. I am so blessed. I am/will be travelling to LAS VEGAS for a week to shoot 2 high budget/upscale music videos. Both music videos are/will be a surprise. Clue: The artists are both well-established/known. Stay tuned! •PART 2• Coming tomorrow... It’ll be a bigger and badder announcement. Stay tuned! I did it. I made it. Thank you Allah!

    Mustafa Jan, Salaam, I went through your LinkedIn connections message. If you are sending it to someone who is in non-for-profit organization project management or in Management positions which is matching to your MBA. It looks perfect! In my introductory message, I personally: - Thank the person for accepting my LinkedIn request or if they send me request, I thank him/her for outreaching. - Mention that I am an Administrative and Human Resources professional with many years of work experience, in case my background matching with the person. - Mention the name of the city of I am living (even though it is mention in LinkedIn account) - I usually do not invite the person over a tea or coffee in my initial text. I just mention, I would greatly appreciate, if you could kindly write me best possible way to meet you. Then they may invite you for coffee, communicate through or phone or Skype, zoom, in his/her company etc or they may write you that I am busy in coupe of weeks. Will let you know. - I sometime write my email address at the signature, I think, it all depends to whom you are sending the introductory message.

    Dear friends of LinkedIn, My time on USAID LEARN has come to an end as of Friday, March 27th. I've accepted a position with The Global Knowledge Initiative that I'm absolutely thrilled about and will be starting my new job tomorrow. This picture was taken five years ago at USAID LEARN's first Moving the Needle Conference in 2015. I have learned so much since that day. The most important lesson that I will take with me is to treat your colleagues as whole people, not just employees. Be kind. Share your time and skills generously. See the potential in your colleague's ideas. When we build each other up, we become stronger and smarter together than we are apart. To my colleagues: from the bottom of my heart, thank you for being amazing colleagues and friends over the past five years. It has been a real pleasure working with you and getting to know you in every respect. Being on this team has been one of the most formative experiences of my life - both personally and professionally. I know I’ll carry the things I’ve learned here with me to my next adventure, and I’ll always look back on this experience with a lot of fondness. Big hug, Kat P.S. To learn more about USAID LEARN's work, check out the USAID Learning Lab: https://lnkd.in/gPxD4ff

    USAID Learning Lab

    usaidlearninglab.org
